<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Customize side, alignment, offsets</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Optionally render a pointing arrow</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports custom open and close delays</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Opens on hover only</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Ignored by screen readers</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the hover card correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the hover card package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> hoverCard</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/hover-card&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The hover card package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to start with the hover card open.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>

<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> to control visibility externally.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-open-and-close-delays" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing open and close delays<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-open-and-close-delays"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openDelay</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeDelay</code> to control hover timing.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hoverCard<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="positioning-the-hover-card" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Positioning the hover card<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#positioning-the-hover-card"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code> to control placement and offsets.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hoverCard<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-the-hover-card" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling the hover card<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-the-hover-card"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to prevent it from opening.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hoverCard<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-open-state-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for open state changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-open-state-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the hover card is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">opened</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closed</code>, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> callback is
invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hoverCard<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;hovercard is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token string">&quot;opened&quot;</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for trigger */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for content */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The hover card exposes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute that can be used to style the
hover card based on its open-close state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="arrow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Arrow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can use CSS variables to style the arrow.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for arrow */</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-background</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">white</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token unit">px</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The hover card machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ trigger: string; content: string; positioner: string; arrow: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the popover. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the hover card opens or closes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openDelay</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The duration from when the mouse enters the trigger until the hover card opens.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeDelay</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The duration from when the mouse leaves the trigger or content until the hover card closes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the hover card is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the hover card</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the hover card when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the hover card.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PositioningOptions</code><span class="d_block">The user provided options used to position the popover content</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The hover card <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the hover card is open</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to open the hover card</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">reposition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(options?: Partial&lt;PositioningOptions&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to reposition the popover</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Trigger</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>hover-card</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>trigger</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-placement</kbd></div><span>The placement of the trigger</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Content</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>hover-card</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>content</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-nested</kbd></div><span>popover</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-has-nested</kbd></div><span>popover</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-placement</kbd></div><span>The placement of the content</span></div></div></div></div>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The hover card is intended for mouse users only so will not respond to keyboard
navigation.</p><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/components/hover-card.mdx" class="d_inline-flex ai_center gap_1 textStyle_a fs_sm mt_14"><svg stroke="currentColor" pkg=\"@zag-js/hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"HoverCard\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Customize side, alignment, offsets\n- Optionally render a pointing arrow\n- Supports custom open and close delays\n- Opens on hover only\n- Ignored by screen readers\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the hover card package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"hover-card/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the hover card correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the hover card package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as hoverCard from \"@zag-js/hover-card\"\n```\n\nThe hover card package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"hover-card/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial state\n\nSet `defaultOpen` to `true` to start with the hover card open.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled open state\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` to control visibility externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing open and close delays\n\nUse `openDelay` and `closeDelay` to control hover timing.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  openDelay: 300,\n  closeDelay: 150,\n})\n```\n\n### Positioning the hover card\n\nUse `positioning` to control placement and offsets.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  positioning: {\n    placement: \"bottom-start\",\n    offset: { mainAxis: 8, crossAxis: 4 },\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling the hover card\n\nSet `disabled` to `true` to prevent it from opening.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for open state changes\n\nWhen the hover card is `opened` or `closed`, the `onOpenChange` callback is\ninvoked.\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    console.log(\"hovercard is:\", details.open ? \"opened\" : \"closed\")\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for trigger */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"] {\n  /* styles for content */\n}\n```\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nThe hover card exposes a `data-state` attribute that can be used to style the\nhover card based on its open-close state.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n```\n\n### Arrow\n\nYou can use CSS variables to style the arrow.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  /* styles for arrow */\n  --arrow-background: white;\n  --arrow-size: 8px;\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe hover card machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe hover card `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"hover-card\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\nThe hover card is intended for mouse users only so will not respond to keyboard\nnavigation."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Hover Card\",\"description\":\"Using the hover-card machine in your
